
namespace = modern_missil

country_event = {
	id = modern_missil.9
	title = modern_missil.9.t
	desc = modern_missil.9.d
	picture = MISSILE_RANGE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}

	

	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.9.a
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.1
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.1.cansel
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
	}
}


country_event = {
	id = modern_missil.1
	title = modern_missil.1.t
	desc = modern_missil.1.d
	picture = MISSILE_RANGE_eventPicture

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Major City
		name = modern_missil.1.a50
		trigger = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_50
				value = 1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_100 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_150 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_250 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_350 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_500 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_700 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1000 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1500 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = use_by_aircoft_carrier
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.50
		}
		set_country_flag = missile_sent_50
	}
	option = { #Center of Trade
		name = modern_missil.1.a100
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_100
				value = 1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_50 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_150 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_250 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_350 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_500 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_700 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1000 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1500 }
		}		
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.100
		}
		set_country_flag = missile_sent_100
	}
	option = { #Fortification
		name = modern_missil.1.a150
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_150
				value = 1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_50 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_100 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_250 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_350 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_500 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_700 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1000 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1500 }
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.150
		}
		set_country_flag = missile_sent_150
	}
	option = { #Port
		name = modern_missil.1.a250
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_250
				value = 1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_50 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_100 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_150 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_350 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_500 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_700 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1000 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1500 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.250
		}
		set_country_flag = missile_sent_250
	}
	option = { #Random Province
		name = modern_missil.1.b350
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_350
				value = 1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_50 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_100 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_150 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_250 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_500 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_700 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1000 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = missile_sent_1500 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = small_satelite_tooltip
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.350
		}
		set_country_flag = missile_sent_350
	}
	option = { #More options

		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_500
				value = 1
			}

country_event = {
	id = modern_missil.50
	title = modern_missil.50.t
	desc = modern_missil.50.d
	picture = MISSILE_RANGE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						sea_superregion = {
							heavy_ships_in_province = root
							#OR = {
							#	controlled_by = root
							#	controller = {
							#		is_subject_of = root
							#	}
							#}
							NOT = {
								province_distance = {
									who = prev
									distance = 50
								}
							}
						}
						any_province = {
							country_or_subject_holds = root
							has_building = mass_transit_system
							OR = {
								controlled_by = root
								controller = {
									is_subject_of = root
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								province_distance = {
									who = prev
									distance = 50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				
				}
				set_province_flag = distance_city_2		
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Major City
		name = modern_missil.1.a50
		trigger = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_50
				value = 1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = use_by_aircoft_carrier
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modifire_distance_50
			duration = -1
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.2
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.1.cansel
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}
}

	id = modern_missil.100
	title = modern_missil.100.t
	desc = modern_missil.100.d
	picture = MISSILE_RANGE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						country_or_subject_holds = root
						has_building = mass_transit_system
						OR = {
							controlled_by = root
							controller = {
								is_subject_of = root
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							province_distance = {
								who = prev
								distance = 100
							}
						}
					}
					is_city = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = distance_city_2
					
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Major City
		name = modern_missil.1.a100
		trigger = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_100
				value = 1
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modifire_distance_100
			duration = -1
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.2
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.1.cansel
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2
				}

			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700

country_event = {
	id = modern_missil.700
	title = modern_missil.700.t
	desc = modern_missil.700.d
	picture = MISSILE_RANGE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						country_or_subject_holds = root
						has_building = mass_transit_system
						OR = {
							controlled_by = root
							controller = {
								is_subject_of = root
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							province_distance = {
								who = prev
								distance = 700
							}
						}
					}
					is_city = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = distance_city_2
					
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Major City
		name = modern_missil.1.a700
		trigger = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_700
				value = 1
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modifire_distance_700
			duration = -1
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.2
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Major City
		name = modern_missil.2.satellite
		trigger = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = missil_700
				value = 1
			}
			event_target:missil_target_country = {
				check_variable = {
					which = satellite_2
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modifire_distance_700
			duration = -1
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_satellite.1
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.1.cansel
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}
}

		}

			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}
}

					add_country_modifier = {
						name = used_missile_8
						duration = 730
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_country_modifier = used_missile

					}

					province_event = {
						id = modern_missil.42
					}
					owner = {
						add_opinion = {
							who = ROOT

				if = {
					limit = {

					}

					country_event = {
						id = modern_missil.9
					}
				}
				every_country = { 
					limit = { NOT = { tag = event_target:missil_target_country } }
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = missile_used
					}
				}
			}
		}

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}
	option = { #Abort Mission
		name = modern_missil.31.b

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100

						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_350
						value = -1
					}
					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_500
						value = -1
					}
					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
					}
					change_variable = {

						value = -1
					}
					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_1000
						value = -1
					}
					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_1500
						value = -1
					}
					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = used_missile } }
					set_global_flag = missile_used
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = used_missile
						duration = 730
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { has_country_modifier = used_missile }
					
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = used_missile_2
						duration = 730
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_country_modifier = used_missile
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_2
					 }
					
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = used_missile_3
						duration = 730
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_country_modifier = used_missile
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_2
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_3
					 }
					
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = used_missile_4
						duration = 730
					}

				else_if = {

						has_country_modifier = used_missile
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_2

						}
					}

					country_event = {
						id = modern_missil.9
					}
				}
				every_country = { 
					limit = { NOT = { tag = event_target:missil_target_country } }
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = missile_used
					}
				}
			}
		}

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}
	option = { #Abort Mission
		name = modern_missil.31.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
		}
		if = {

				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
		}
		if = {

		if = {

			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700

						every_owned_province = {
							limit = { 
								has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
							}
							clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
						}
						every_owned_province = {
							limit = { 
								has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
							}
							clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
						}
					}
					clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
					country_event = {
						id = modern_missil.9
					}
				}
				every_country = { 
					limit = { NOT = { tag = event_target:missil_target_country } }
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = missile_used
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}
	option = { #Abort Mission
		name = modern_missil.31.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
		}
		if = {

		if = {

		}
		if = {

		}
		if = {

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100

			else = {

	}
	option = { #Abort Mission

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country

		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000

	option = { #Abort Mission
		name = modern_missil.31.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}
}

											value = 97
										}
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {	
								check_variable = {
									which = defense_missile_lev
									value = 97
								}
							
								NOT = {
									check_variable = {
										which = defense_missile_lev
										value = 98
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									NOT = {
										check_variable = {
											which = attack_missile_lev
											value = 98
										}
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {	
								check_variable = {
									which = defense_missile_lev
									value = 98
								}
							
								NOT = {
									check_variable = {
										which = defense_missile_lev
										value = 99
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									NOT = {
										check_variable = {
											which = attack_missile_lev
											value = 99
										}
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {	
								check_variable = {
									which = defense_missile_lev
									value = 99
								}
							
								NOT = {
									check_variable = {
										which = defense_missile_lev
										value = 100
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									NOT = {
										check_variable = {
											which = attack_missile_lev
											value = 100
										}
									}
								}
							}
							AND = {	
								check_variable = {
									which = defense_missile_lev
									value = 100
								}

									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									NOT = {
										check_variable = {
											which = attack_missile_lev
											value = 101
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						event_target:missil_target_country = { 
							full_idea_group = defence_missil_research
						}
						event_target:missil_target_country = {
							overlord = { 
								full_idea_group = defence_missil_research
							}
						}
					}
					event_target:missil_target_country = { 
						check_variable = {
							which = missil_50
							value = 1
						}
					}
					event_target:missil_target_province = {
						has_building = road
					}
				}
				event_target:missil_target_province = {
					province_event = {
						id = they_cant_set_atom.2
					}
				}
				event_target:missil_target_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_50
						value = -1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = missil_50
						value = -1

					remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50

			else = {
				if = {

						has_country_modifier = used_missile_4

					 }

						has_country_modifier = used_missile_2
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_3
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_4
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_5
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_6
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_7
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_8
						has_country_modifier = used_missile_9
					 }
					
					add_country_modifier = {

						duration = 730
					}
				}
				
				event_target:missil_target_province = {
					
					province_event = {
						id = modern_missil.902
					}
					owner = {

							who = ROOT
							modifier = missile_us

				if = {
					limit = {

								value = 1

								value = 1
							}
							check_variable = {

								value = 1

							check_variable = {

								value = 1
							}

					event_target:missil_target_country = {
						every_owned_province = {
							limit = { 
								has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
							}
							clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
						}
						every_owned_province = {
							limit = { 
								has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
							}
							clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
						}
					}
					clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
					country_event = {
						id = modern_missil.9
					}
				}
				every_country = { 
					limit = { NOT = { tag = event_target:missil_target_country } }
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = missile_used
						}
				}
			}
		}	

		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
	}
	option = { #Abort Mission
		name = modern_missil.31.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_province
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}

province_event = {
	id = modern_missil.41
	title = modern_missil.3.t
	desc = modern_missil.41.d
	picture = MISSILE_BOMB_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		
		kill_units = {
			who = owner
			amount = 1
		}
		random_list = {
			33 = { add_base_tax = -1 }
			33 = { add_base_production = -1 }
			34 = { add_base_manpower = -1 }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = province_missile
			duration = 730
		}
		remove_building = mass_transit_system
		owner = {
			add_casus_belli = {
				type = cb_missile_attack
				target = FROM
				months = 120
			}
			overlord = {
				add_casus_belli = {
					type = cb_missile_attack_military_base
					target = FROM
					months = 120
				}
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { #
		name = modern_missil.3.a
		add_devastation = 5
		owner = { add_war_exhaustion = 0.05 }	
	}	
}

province_event = {
	id = modern_missil.502
	title = modern_missil.3.t
	desc = modern_missil.502.d
	picture = MISSILE_BOMB_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		
		kill_units = {
			who = owner
			amount = 1
		}
		random_list = {
			33 = { add_base_tax = -1 }
			33 = { add_base_production = -1 }
			34 = { add_base_manpower = -1 }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = province_missile
			duration = 730
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = fort_18th
			}
			remove_building = fort_18th
			add_building = fort_17th
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = fort_17th
			}
			remove_building = fort_17th
			add_building = fort_16th
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = fort_16th
			}
			remove_building = fort_16th
			add_building = fort_15th
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = fort_15th
			}
			remove_building = fort_15th
			add_building = fort_et
		}
		else = {
			remove_building = fort_et
		}
		owner = {
			add_casus_belli = {
				type = cb_missile_attack
				target = FROM
				months = 120
			}
			overlord = {
				add_casus_belli = {
					type = cb_missile_attack_military_base
					target = FROM
					months = 120
				}
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { #
		name = modern_missil.3.a
		add_devastation = 5
		owner = { add_war_exhaustion = 0.05 }	
	}	
}

country_event = {
	id = modern_missil.4
	title = modern_missil.2.t
	desc = modern_missil.2.d
	picture = NUCLEAR_TARGET_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					any_owned_province = { 
						controlled_by = event_target:missil_target_country 
						has_building = highway  has_province_flag = distance_city_2 NOT = { has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2 }
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_building = highway has_province_flag = distance_city_2 NOT = { has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2 } }
					save_event_target_as = anti_atomic_bomb
					set_province_flag = distance_city_1_2					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					any_owned_province = { 
						controlled_by = event_target:missil_target_country 
						has_building = road  has_province_flag = distance_city_2 NOT = { has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2 }
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_building = road has_province_flag = distance_city_2 NOT = { has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2 } }
					save_event_target_as = anti_missile
					set_province_flag = distance_city_1_2					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					any_owned_province = { 
						controlled_by = event_target:missil_target_country

					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {

			}

		trigger = { 
			has_saved_event_target = constable_city 
		}
		event_target:constable_city = {
			custom_tooltip = SET_AS_MISSILE_TARGET
			save_event_target_as = missil_target_province
		}
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.36
		}
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = { #Random Province
		name = modern_missil.2.g
		goto = training_fields_city

				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2

		event_target:missil_target_country = {

	option = { #More options
		name = modern_missil.2.l
		country_event = {
			id = modern_missil.4
		}
	}
	option = { #Cancel
		name = modern_missil.2.m
		event_target:missil_target_country = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_2 					
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_2
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
				}
				clr_province_flag = distance_city_1_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_350
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_700
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
			}
			remove_country_modifier = modifire_distance_1500
		}
		clear_global_event_target = missil_target_country
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_50
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_100
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_150
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_250
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_350
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_500
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_700
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1000
		clr_country_flag = missile_sent_1500
	}
